VBA MACRO Sheet19.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet19'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Const KIRPICH_TC = 1
Const KENT_TC = 2

Private Function checkdata()
 Dim isOK As Boolean
 Dim Cad As String
 Dim Area As Double
 Dim TcOption As Byte
 Dim TcMethod As Byte
 Dim CN As Double
 
 Cad = "Error, please check:" & Chr(13) & Chr(13)
 isOK = True
 Area = Range("F6").value
 If (Area <= 0) Then
   isOK = False
   Cad = Cad & "Total drainage area " & Chr(13)
 End If
 
 TcOption = Range("K13").value
 If (TcOption = 1) Then
   Tc = Range("F9").value
 Else
   TcMethod = Range("K16").value
   If (TcMethod = KENT_TC) Then
     CN = Range("I17").value
     If (CN < 1 Or CN > 100) Then
      isOK = False
      Cad = Cad & "Curver Number Value"
     End If
   End If
   Tc = Range("I19").value
   
 End If
 
 If (Tc <= 0 Or Tc > 50) Then
   isOK = False
   Cad = Cad & "Time of concentration " & Chr(13)
 End If
 
 If (isOK = False) Then MsgBox Cad, vbExclamation
 
 checkdata = isOK
End Function

Private Sub CommandButton1_Click()
 Module1.GotoMain
End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton2_Click()
 Dim FName As String
 'FName = Module1.W5OpenFile_Watershed(1)
 FName = Module1.OpenFileDialog("Watershed Timing data file (*.wt), *.wt")
 If (FName <> "") Then
   ReadWatershedFile FName
 End If
End Sub


Sub ReadWatershedFile(NFile As String)
Dim Slope As Double
Dim Channel As Double
Dim Area As Double
Dim CN As Double
Dim Tc As Double
Dim D1, D2, D3
Dim WName As String
Dim MethodTc As Integer

'Open NFile For Input As #1
'Input #1, WName
'Input #1, Slope, Channel, Tc, MethodTc
'Input #1, Area, CN
'Close #1

ModuleIO.ReadWatershedInfo NFile, WName, Slope, Channel, Tc, MethodTc, Area, CN

Range("F4").value = WName
Range("I13").value = Slope
Range("I15").value = Channel
Range("F9").value = Tc

Range("F6").value = Area
Range("I17").value = CN
Range("K13").value = MethodTc
End Sub

Private Sub SaveWatershedFile(NFile As String)
Dim Slope As Double
Dim Channel As Double
Dim Area As Double
Dim CN As Double
Dim Tc As Double
Dim D1, D2, D3
Dim WName As String
Dim MethodTc As Integer

WName = Range("F4").value
Slope = Range("I13").value
Channel = Range("I15").value
Tc = Range("F9").value
Area = Range("F6").value
CN = Range("I17").value
MethodTc = Range("K13").value

ModuleIO.SaveWatershedInfo NFile, WName, Slope, Channel, Tc, MethodTc, Area, CN

'Open NFile For Output As #1
'Write #1, WName
'Write #1, Slope, Channel, Tc, MethodTc
'Write #1, Area, CN
'Close #1
End Sub


Private Sub CommandButton3_Click()

 FileName = Range("F4").value
 FileName = Module1.SaveFileDialog(FileName, "Watershed Timing data file (*.wt), *.wt")
 If (FileName <> "") Then
  SaveWatershedFile FileName
 End If
End Sub


Private Sub Copy_Temporal_Data(Dir As Byte)
 Dim page1 As String
 Dim page2 As String
 
 page1 = "watershed2"
 page2 = "tmpData"
 
 CopyData Dir, page1, "F4", page2, "E16" 'Name
 CopyData Dir, page1, "F6", page2, "E28" 'Total Area
 CopyData Dir, page1, "F9", page2, "E19" 'TC given value
 CopyData Dir, page1, "K13", page2, "E18" 'TC Method (Given or Calculated)
 CopyData Dir, page1, "K16", page2, "E20" 'TC Formula for calculation
 CopyData Dir, page1, "I13", page2, "E23" 'Slope
 CopyData Dir, page1, "I15", page2, "E24" 'Length Channel
 CopyData Dir, page1, "I17", page2, "E27" 'CN
 
 'SIMAS Method
 CopyData Dir, page1, "I24", page2, "I18" 'Width
 CopyData Dir, page1, "I26", page2, "I19" 'Slope
 If (Dir = 0) Then
  CopyData Dir, page1, "I30", page2, "I20" 'TL
  CopyData Dir, page1, "I19", page2, "E25" 'TL
 End If
 
End Sub

VBA MACRO ModuleIO.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/ModuleIO'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 


Sub SaveWatershedInfo(NFile As String, WName As String, Slope As Double, Channel As Double, Tc As Double, MethodTc As Integer, Area As Double, CN As Double)
Dim isProject As Boolean

isProject = (NFile = "")
  
  If (isProject = False) Then
   Open NFile For Output As #1
  End If
  Write #1, WName
  Write #1, Slope, Channel, Tc, MethodTc
  Write #1, Area, CN
  If (isProject = False) Then Close #1
End Sub

Sub ReadWatershedInfo(NFile As String, ByRef WName As String, ByRef Slope As Double, ByRef Channel As Double, ByRef Tc As Double, ByRef MethodTc As Integer, ByRef Area As Double, ByRef CN As Double)
Dim isProject As Boolean

isProject = (NFile = "")
If (isProject = False) Then
  Open NFile For Input As #1
End If
Input #1, WName
Input #1, Slope, Channel, Tc, MethodTc
Input #1, Area, CN
If (isProject = False) Then Close #1
End Sub

Sub SaveMyProject()
 'SaveWatershedInfo "testfile.txt", "watershed1", 19, 3000, 0.4, 1, 1000, 84
 Open "demo2.txt" For Output As #1
 SaveWatershedInfo "", "watershed1", 19, 3000, 0.4, 1, 1000, 84
 Close #1
End Sub

Sub Macro3()
Attribute Macro3.VB_ProcData.VB_Invoke_Func = " \n14"
'
' Macro3 Macro
'

'
    Range("O8").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "a="
    Range("M10").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "f="
    With ActiveCell.Characters(Start:=1, Length:=0).Font
        .Name = "Arial"
        .FontStyle = "Regular"
        .Size = 10
        .Strikethrough = False
        .Superscript = False
        .Subscript = False
        .OutlineFont = False
        .Shadow = False
        .Underline = xlUnderlineStyleNone
        .ColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .ThemeFont = xlThemeFontNone
    End With
    With ActiveCell.Characters(Start:=1, Length:=1).Font
        .Name = "Calibri"
        .FontStyle = "Regular"
        .Size = 10
        .Strikethrough = False
        .Superscript = False
        .Subscript = False
        .OutlineFont = False
        .Shadow = False
        .Underline = xlUnderlineStyleNone
        .ColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .ThemeFont = xlThemeFontNone
    End With
    With ActiveCell.Characters(Start:=2, Length:=1).Font
        .Name = "Arial"
        .FontStyle = "Regular"
        .Size = 10
        .Strikethrough = False
        .Superscript = False
        .Subscript = False
        .OutlineFont = False
        .Shadow = False
        .Underline = xlUnderlineStyleNone
        .ColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .ThemeFont = xlThemeFontNone
    End With
    Range("M11").Select
End Sub

Sub help_DIF()

Dim Cad As String

Cad = "Distributed infiltration capacity:   Parameter Selection and Background"
Cad = Cad & "Parameter Selection   Responsible selection of muf  for use in the"
Cad = Cad & "model here is a choice left to the judgment and"
Cad = Cad & "experience of the user, as well as local conditions."
Cad = Cad & "There are no formally developed  authoritative tables for muf ;"
Cad = Cad & "use of the technique here is developmental. However, as an average,"
Cad = Cad & "steady-state infiltration velocity it is related to point equilibrium rates found elsewhere."
Cad = Cad & "In this light, the following are offered for suggestions, guide, and perspective only."
Cad = "Ks is the saturated hydraulic conductivity, or the steady-state rate found in some ideal"

 TextBox1.Text = Cad
End Sub

  frHelp.Show

in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet23'

Dim ComeFrom As Byte
'0=from Watershed, 1=from Rainfall Excess 0.2, 2=Rainfall Excess 0.05

Sub SetFrom_Origin(id As Byte)
 ComeFrom = id
End Sub

Private Function Check_CNValues() As Boolean
Dim isOK As Boolean
Dim isGoodRow As Boolean
Dim page As String
Dim NRows As Integer
Dim Val1
Dim Val2
Dim Cad As String

Cad = ""
isOK = True
page = "CNS"
NRows = 0

  For I = 1 To 20
      Val1 = Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 5).value
      Val2 = Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 7).value
      If (Val1 <> "" Or Val2 <> "") Then
        isGoodRow = True
        If (IsNumeric(Val1) And IsNumeric(Val2)) Then
           If (Val1 <= 0) Then
             Cad = Cad & Chr(13) & "Check Area at row # " & I
             isOK = False
             isGoodRow = False
           End If
           
           If (Val2 <= 1 Or Val2 > 100) Then
             Cad = Cad & Chr(13) & "Check CN Value at row # " & I
             isOK = False
             isGoodRow = False
           End If
           
          Else
           Cad = Cad & Chr(13) & "Check Values at row # " & I
           isOK = False
           isGoodRow = False
        End If
        
        If (isGoodRow = True) Then NRows = NRows + 1
      End If 'there is something
 Next I
 
 If (NRows < 1) Then
   Cad = "You must input correct data" & Chr(13) & Cad
   isOK = False
 End If
 
 If (isOK = False) Then MsgBox Cad, vbExclamation
 
 Check_CNValues = isOK
End Function

Private Function GetHowMany() As Integer
Dim page As String
Dim NRows As Integer
Dim Val1
Dim Val2

page = "CNS"
NRows = 0

  For I = 1 To 20
      Val1 = Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 5).value
      Val2 = Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 7).value
      If (IsNumeric(Val1) And IsNumeric(Val2)) Then
      If (Val1 > 0) And (Val2 > 0) Then
        NRows = NRows + 1
      End If
      End If
 Next I
 
 GetHowMany = NRows
End Function


Private Sub CopyFromTMP()
'Get a Copy of Data from tmpData
 Worksheets("CNS").Range("E6:G25").value = Worksheets("tmpData").Range("W5:Y24").value
End Sub

Private Sub CopyToTMP()
'Places a Copy of Data at tmpData
 Worksheets("tmpData").Range("W5:Y24").value = Worksheets("CNS").Range("E6:G25").value
End Sub

Private Sub AcceptData()
Dim page As String
Dim NRows As Integer

 NRows = GetHowMany
 
 page = "tmpData"
 If (NRows > 0) Then
 Worksheets(page).Range("E27").value = Range("L17").value 'CN
 Worksheets(page).Range("E28").value = Range("L15").value 'Area
 CopyToTMP
 If (ComeFrom > 0) Then
   Sheet14.AcceptRE_Method "accept"
   Module1.GotoMain
 Else
  GotoWatershed1 False
 End If
Else
  MsgBox "You must input some information", vbInformation
End If
End Sub


Private Sub CommandButton1_Click()

Dim isOK As Boolean
 
isOK = Check_CNValues
If (isOK = True) Then AcceptData
End Sub

Sub ReadUHFile(NFile As String)

Dim NumUH As Integer
Dim Area As Double
Dim CN As Double
Dim page As String

page = "CNS"
Worksheets(page).Range("E6:G25").value = ""

Open NFile For Input As #1
Input #1, NumUH
For I = 1 To NumUH
   Input #1, Area, CN
   Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 5).value = Area
   Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 7).value = CN
 Next I
Close #1
End Sub


Sub SaveUHFile(NFile As String, NRows As Integer)

Dim page As String
Dim Val1 As Variant
Dim Val2 As Variant

page = "CNS"

Open NFile For Output As #1
Write #1, NRows

For I = 1 To 20
     Val1 = Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 5).value
     Val2 = Worksheets(page).Cells(5 + I, 7).value
            
      If (IsNumeric(Val1) And IsNumeric(Val2)) Then
      If (Val1 >= 0) And (Val2 >= 0) Then
        Write #1, Val1, Val2
      End If
      End If
 Next I

Close #1

End Sub





Private Sub CommandButton2_Click()
 Module1.W5OpenFile_UH
End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton3_Click()
Dim NRows As Integer

 If (Check_CNValues = True) Then
 NRows = GetHowMany
 If (NRows > 0) Then
  Module1.W5SaveFile_UH NRows
 Else
  MsgBox "There is not information to save", vbExclamation
 End If
 End If
End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton5_Click()
Dim CN
Dim R As Integer
Dim C As Integer

C = ActiveCell.Column
R = ActiveCell.Row

If (R >= 6 And R <= 25) Then

  Load frCN
  CN = frCN.GetCNTable()
  Unload frCN

  If (CN > -1) Then
   Cells(R, 7).value = CN
  End If
 End If
End Sub

Dim CNA, CNB, CNC, CND, CNSelected


Private Sub SetVals(a, b, C, d)
 CNA = a
 CNB = b
 CNC = C
 CND = d
End Sub

Private Sub getCNS(index)
  If (index = 0) Then SetVals 77, 86, 91, 94
  If (index = 1) Then SetVals 72, 81, 88, 91
  If (index = 2) Then SetVals 67, 78, 85, 89
  If (index = 3) Then SetVals 70, 79, 84, 88
  If (index = 4) Then SetVals 65, 75, 82, 86
  If (index = 5) Then SetVals 66, 74, 80, 82
  If (index = 6) Then SetVals 62, 71, 78, 81
  If (index = 7) Then SetVals 65, 76, 84, 88
  If (index = 8) Then SetVals 63, 75, 83, 87
  If (index = 9) Then SetVals 63, 74, 82, 85
  If (index = 10) Then SetVals 61, 73, 81, 84
  If (index = 11) Then SetVals 61, 72, 79, 82
  If (index = 12) Then SetVals 59, 70, 78, 81
  If (index = 13) Then SetVals 66, 77, 85, 89
  If (index = 14) Then SetVals 58, 72, 81, 85
  If (index = 15) Then SetVals 58, 72, 81, 85
  If (index = 16) Then SetVals 64, 75, 83, 85
  If (index = 17) Then SetVals 55, 69, 78, 83
  If (index = 18) Then SetVals 63, 73, 80, 83
  If (index = 19) Then SetVals 68, 79, 86, 89
  If (index = 20) Then SetVals 49, 69, 79, 84
  If (index = 21) Then SetVals 39, 61, 74, 80
  If (index = 22) Then SetVals 47, 67, 81, 88
  If (index = 23) Then SetVals 25, 59, 75, 83
  If (index = 24) Then SetVals 6, 35, 70, 79
  If (index = 25) Then SetVals 30, 58, 71, 78
  If (index = 26) Then SetVals 45, 66, 77, 83
  If (index = 27) Then SetVals 36, 60, 73, 79
  If (index = 28) Then SetVals 25, 55, 70, 77
  If (index = 29) Then SetVals 59, 74, 82, 86
  If (index = 30) Then SetVals 72, 82, 87, 89
  If (index = 31) Then SetVals 74, 84, 90, 92
End Sub

Private Function getCNCad(index)
Dim Cad As String
  getCNS index
  getCNCad = "      " & CNA & "  " & CNB & "  " & CNC & "  " & CND
End Function

Sub Macro17()
Attribute Macro17.VB_ProcData.VB_Invoke_Func = " \n14"
'
' Macro17 Macro
'

'
    ActiveSheet.ChartObjects("Chart 1").Activate
    ActiveChart.PlotArea.Select
    ActiveSheet.ChartObjects("Chart 1").Activate
    ActiveChart.Axes(xlValue).AxisTitle.Select
    Range("D1").Select
    ActiveSheet.ChartObjects("Chart 1").Activate
    ActiveChart.Axes(xlValue).AxisTitle.Select
    ActiveSheet.ChartObjects("Chart 1").Activate
    ActiveChart.Axes(xlValue, xlPrimary).AxisTitle.Text = "Q (ft^3/2)"
End Sub
Sub Macro18()
Attribute Macro18.VB_ProcData.VB_Invoke_Func = " \n14"
'
' Macro18 Macro
'

'
    Range("C1").Select
    ActiveCell.FormulaR1C1 = "."
    With ActiveCell.Characters(Start:=1, Length:=1).Font
        .Name = "Arial"
        .FontStyle = "Regular"
        .Size = 10
        .Strikethrough = False
        .Superscript = False
        .Subscript = False
        .OutlineFont = False
        .Shadow = False
        .Underline = xlUnderlineStyleNone
        .ColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .ThemeFont = xlThemeFontNone
    End With
    Range("C2").Select
End Sub

VBA MACRO frCover.frm 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/frCover'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 

Private isUMetric As Boolean
Private XMu As Double

Private Sub SetVegetative(value As Double, isEnabled As Boolean)
  TextBox1.value = value
  TextBox1.Enabled = isEnabled
  If (isEnabled = True) Then
  TextBox1.BackColor = &H80000005
  Else
  TextBox1.BackColor = &HE0E0E0
  End If
  
End Sub


Private Sub Calculate()
 Dim CG As Double
 Dim CC As Double
 Dim Keb As Double
 Dim Ke As Double
 
 Dim Vegetative As Double
 Dim Clay As Double
 Dim Mu As Double
 Dim ErrorList As String
 
 ErrorList = ""
 
 Vegetative = TextBox1.value
 If (Vegetative < 0 Or Vegative > 1) Then ErrorList = "Vegetative Fraction"
 
 CG = TextBox2.value
 If (CG < 0 Or CG > 1) Then ErrorList = ErrorList + Chr(13) + "Ground Cover Fraction"
 CC = TextBox3.value
 If (CC < 0 Or CC > 1) Then ErrorList = ErrorList + Chr(13) + "Canopy Cover Fraction"
 Clay = TextBox4.value
 If (Clay < 0 Or Clay > 1) Then ErrorList = ErrorList + Chr(13) + "Clay Fraction"
 
 
 If (ErrorList = "") Then
  Keb = 0.174 - 1.45 * Clay + 2.975 * CG + 0.923 * CC
  Keb = (1 / 3) * Exp(Keb)
  Ke = Keb * Vegetative
  Mu = 8 * Exp(0.0912 * Ke)
  CommandButton2.Enabled = True
  
  TextBox5.value = Format(Keb, "#,##0.000")
  TextBox8.value = Format(Keb / 25.4, "#,##0.000")
  TextBox6.value = Format(Ke, "#,##0.000")
  TextBox9.value = Format(Ke / 25.4, "#,##0.000")
  TextBox7.value = Format(Mu, "#,##0.000")
  TextBox10.value = Format(Mu / 25.4, "#,##0.000")
  
  If (isUMetric = True) Then
   XMu = Mu
  Else
   XMu = Mu / 25.4
  End If
 Else
  CommandButton2.Enabled = False
  ErrorList = "Please check the following values: " + Chr(13) + ErrorList
  MsgBox ErrorList
 End If
 

End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton1_Click()
  Calculate
End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton2_Click()
 frCover.Hide
 
End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton3_Click()
 XMu = -1
 frCover.Hide
End Sub

Private Sub CommandButton4_Click()
Module1.W5Help "W5Cover.pdf"
End Sub

Private Sub OptionButton1_Click()
  SetVegetative 0.8, False
End Sub

Private Sub OptionButton2_Click()
 SetVegetative 1, False
End Sub

Private Sub OptionButton3_Click()
 SetVegetative 1.2, False
End Sub

Private Sub OptionButton4_Click()
 SetVegetative 1, True
End Sub




Private Sub UserForm_Initialize()
 OptionButton1_Click
 CommandButton2.Enabled = False
End Sub

  isUMetric = isMetric
  frCover.Show
  CoverDlg = XMu
End Function

+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
|Type      |Keyword             |Description                                  |
+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
|AutoExec  |Workbook_Open       |Runs when the Excel Workbook is opened       |
|AutoExec  |Workbook_BeforeClose|Runs when the Excel Workbook is closed       |
|AutoExec  |CommandButton1_Click|Runs when the file is opened and ActiveX     |
|          |                    |objects trigger events                       |
|Suspicious|Open                |May open a file                              |
|Suspicious|Write               |May write to a file (if combined with Open)  |
|Suspicious|Output              |May write to a file (if combined with Open)  |
|Suspicious|Print #             |May write to a file (if combined with Open)  |
|Suspicious|vbNormalNoFocus     |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
